For S=256, `k` iterates 0..3 (line 469), so `k*64 + key_load_col_id*4` covers 0..63, 64..127, 128..191, 192..255. **The read side is OK.** Only the **write side** (lines 440–443) is problematic — it must also cover the full S range.\n\n**Required fix for lines 440–443 (value store to LDS):**\nAdd a loop or unrolled second set of stores for the upper half of S. For example:\n```cpp\nfor (int half = 0; half < S / 128; half++) {\n    *(bfloat16x8*)(&cur_v_buff_lds[(key_load_row_id + 0*4) * S + half * 64 + key_load_col_id * 8]) = v_reg_caches[4*n + 0];\n    // ... same for rows 1, 2, 3\n}\n```\nBut this requires rethinking the data arrangement since `v_reg_caches` loads only 8 bf16 per load (each `global_load_dwordx4<bfloat16x8>`). One load suffices.\n- For **S=256**: this covers only the first 128 of 256 elements. **Second load needed.**\n\n**Required change for S=256** (line 340 and friends):\nEither:\n- Add a second set of loads at offset `+ 128 * sizeof(__bf16)`, or\n- Double `v_reg_caches` size (from `KV_PART_SIZE_WARP/4` to `KV_PART_SIZE_WARP/2`) and load two chunks per value.\n\nThe same issue applies to key loads at **line 335**:\n```cpp\nauto offset = k_idxs[n] * (HK * S * sizeof(__bf16)) + 8 * sizeof(__bf16) * key_load_col_id;\nk_reg_caches[n] = global_load_dwordx4<bfloat16x8>(key_cache, offset);\n```\n- Same problem: 16 cols × 8 bf16 = 128 bf16, half of S=256.\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table of All Required Changes\n\n| # | Line(s) | File | Current (S=128) | Required for S=256 | Category |\n|---|---------|------|-----------------|--------------------|----------|\n| 0 | 186 | `pa.cpp` | `#define S 128` | `#define S 256` | Definition |\n| 1 | 335, 340 | `pa.cpp` | `global_load_dwordx4<bfloat16x8>` at `key_load_col_id * 8` (loads 128 bf16 per key) | **Must load 256 bf16 per key.** Need 2 loads per key or double the number of `k_reg_caches`/`v_reg_caches` entries and add second offset `+ 128*sizeof(__bf16)`. | Global memory load |\n| 2 | 440–443 | `pa.cpp` | Value store to LDS writes 128 bf16 per row (16 cols × 8 bf16) | **Must write 256 bf16 per row.** Add a second set of writes offset by 64 (in bf16x8 units) or add a loop. | LDS value store |\n| 3 | 534 | `pa.cpp` | `((bfloat16x2*)(share_buf.get_out_buf(0) + m_token_id * S))[(m_token_id ^ (lane_id / 2)) * 2 + (lane_id & 1)]` | Change to `bfloat16x4`, group by `lane_id/4`, index by `lane_id & 3`, stride `*4`. | LDS final read (cross-warp reduce) |\n| 4 | 536–538 | `pa.cpp` | `float32x2 out_v;
